  • 📝 $.orderedItem[2].orderedItem.superEvent.eventStatus: Data consumers will assume the eventStatus is scheduled if not specified or invalid.

✅ Booking should succeed if Broker and Customer are included in Order, because we are in ResellerBroker mode >> Assert Opportunity Capacity (after B)
